country_event = { #开局
	id = hnn.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hnn.1" }
	title = hnn.1.t
	desc = hnn.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HNN_map

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = hnn.1.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = HNN
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = ANQ
			white_peace = CHI
			white_peace = SQI
			country_event = { 
				id = hnn.2 
				days = 3 
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = CHI.midgame.814
				days = 60 
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = CHI.midgame.813
				days = 450 
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = CHI.midgame.811
				days = 300
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = CHI.midgame.810
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #省议会问题
	id = hnn.2

	id = hnn.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hnn.4" }
	title = hnn.4.t
	desc = hnn.4.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = hnn.4.a
		add_political_power = -50
		remove_ideas = HNN_a_democratic_province
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.18
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = HNN_revolution
			activate_mission = HNN_yi_guan_dao
			country_event = { 
				id = hnnwar.1 
				days = 5 
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = hnn.10
	title = hnn.10.t
	desc = {
		text = hnn.10.d_zhili
		trigger = { 
			has_country_leader = { name = "汤芗铭" ruling_only = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hnn.10.d_fed
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "谭延闿" ruling_only = yes }

				}

				has_country_leader = { name = "赵恒惕" ruling_only = yes }

		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_HNN_new_army_soldiers

	option = {

		name = hnn.10.a
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #石启贵的上书
	id = hnn.13
	title = hnn.13.t
	desc = hnn.13.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes 

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			HNN_lian_sheng_goverment = yes
			has_completed_focus = HNN_victory_of_the_united_front
		}
	}

	option = { 
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event hnn.13 option hnn.13.a"
		name = hnn.13.a
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = HNN_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = HNN_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
				days = -20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = HNN_industrial_reform_mission_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = HNN_industrial_reform_mission_timer
				days = -20
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event hnn.13 option hnn.13.b"
		name = hnn.13.b
		add_political_power = 40
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = HNN_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = HNN_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
				days = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = HNN_industrial_reform_mission_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = HNN_industrial_reform_mission_timer
				days = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = hnn.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hnn.55" }

		}

		}
	}
}

			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hnn.66.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #accept
		name = hnn.66.a
		hidden_effect = {
			HNN = {
				country_event = {
					id = hnn.67
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			HNN = {
				country_event = {
					id = hnn.68
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = { #选举开始
	id = hnnelection.1
	title = hnnelection.1.t
	desc = hnnelection.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_official_announcement

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event hnnelection.1 option hnnelection.1.a"
		name = hnnelection.1.a
		set_country_flag = HNN_electionsstarted
		add_political_power = 20
		set_variable = { hnn_tan_popularity = 3 }
		set_variable = { hnn_zhao_popularity = 1 }
		set_variable = { hnn_chen_popularity = 1 }
		HNN_election_update_percentage_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_tang_campaign_tan }
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_tang_campaign_zhao }
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_tang_campaign_cheng }
				}
				random_list = {
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_demacry_campaign_zhao }
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_xiangxi_campaign_chen }
					33 = { activate_mission = HNN_all_campaign_tan }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { 
				id = hnnelection.2 
				days = 7 
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = hnnzhili.1.a

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HNN_path
						option = HNN_TSZ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HNN_path
						option = HNN_ZJP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HNN_path
						option = HNN_CQ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HNN_path
						option = HNN_HJ
					}
				}
			}
		}

			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = HNN_ye_kaixin
			retire_character = HNN_zhao_hengti
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat

				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = POLITICS_HNN_tang_xiangming_DESC

					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				HNN_a_democratic_province_2
				HNN_a_democratic_province_3
				HNN_peasant_support_weak
				HNN_peasant_support_growing
				HNN_peasant_support_strong

				HNN_basic_welfare
				HNN_robust_academic_infrastructure
				HNN_rights_guaranteed

				HNN_bill_of_rights
				HNN_democratic_traditions
				HNN_diarchy_influence_curbbed
				HNN_democratic_stronghold
			}
			country_event = hnnzhili.2
			if = {#CHI的反应
				limit = { 
					CHI = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					country_event = hnnwar.4
				}
			}

				limit = {

					has_global_flag = QIE_manchu_restoration

					}

					SZC = { 
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					}

					country_event = { 
						id = qiefor.113 
						days = 3 
					}

					days = 2 
				}
			}
		}

	id = hnnshenbing.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hnnshenbing.1" }
	title = hnnshenbing.1.t
	desc = hnnshenbing.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = hnnshenbing.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HNN_shen_bing_victory_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = HNN_a_democratic_province
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = HNN_GT
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.40
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			add_ideas = HNN_sabotaged_industry
			add_natpop_to_coalition = yes
			set_country_flag = HNN_shen_bing_victory
			if = {
				limit = { 
					CHI = {
						has_character = HNN_he_long
					}
				}
				HNN_he_long = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_leader = yes
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = {
							large = GFX_Portrait_Hunan_He_Long_shen_bing
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = POLITICS_HNN_HE_LONG_SHEN_BING_DESC
							ideology = comrades_coast_subtype
							traits = {
								CHN_Syndicalists_aligned
							}
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				HNN_he_long = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_leader = yes
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = {
							large = GFX_Portrait_Hunan_He_Long_shen_bing
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = POLITICS_HNN_HE_LONG_SHEN_BING_DESC
							ideology = comrades_coast_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			HNN_geng_biao = { HNN_recruit_characters_effect = yes }
			HNN_Xu_Si_You = { HNN_recruit_characters_effect = yes }
			HNN_geng_biao = { HNN_recruit_characters_effect = yes }
			HNN_Yuan_Wen_Cai = { HNN_recruit_characters_effect = yes }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = HNN_totalist_party_shen_long_long
				name = HNN_totalist_party_shen_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = HNN_national_populist_party_shen_long_long
				name = HNN_national_populist_party_shen_long
			}

			retire_character = HNN_tang_xiangming
			retire_character = HNN_yuan_zuming
			retire_character = HNN_chen_quzhen
			retire_character = HNN_tian_yingzhao
			retire_character = HNN_ye_kaixin
			retire_character = HNN_zhao_hengti
		
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = SQI_lu_jin }
				retire_character = SQI_lu_jin
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = SQI_zhang_jingyao }
				retire_character = SQI_zhang_jingyao
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = QIE_manchu_restoration } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = qiefor.141 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { SZC = { is_ruled_by_pro_zhili = yes } }
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { is_character = HNN_tang_xiangming }
					set_nationality = SZC
					unit_leader_event = qieflavor.14
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_character = SQI_lu_jin 
					}
					random_unit_leader = {
						limit = { is_character = SQI_lu_jin }
						set_nationality = SZC
						unit_leader_event = qieflavor.14
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_character = SQI_lu_jin 
					}
					random_unit_leader = {
						limit = { is_character = SQI_lu_jin }
						set_nationality = SZC
						unit_leader_event = qieflavor.14
					}
				}
			}
			QIE_ma_dengying_flees_effect = yes

			set_party_name ={
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = SHC_totalist_party_PLE_long
				name = SHC_totalist_party_PLE
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hungong.79" }
	title = hungong.79.t
	desc = hungong.79.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {#康生
		name = hungong.79.a
		SHC_Kang_Sheng = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = { 
					desc = Kang_Shen_DESC
					ideology = socialist_security_state_subtype
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name =  HNN_totalist_party_proc_k_long
			name =  HNN_totalist_party_proc_k
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = HNN_PROC_K
		HNN_fcations_change = yes 
		add_ideas = HNN_di_kang_de_da_zong1
		add_ideas = LEC_kang_sheng_hog
	}

	option = {#戴笠
		name = hungong.79.b
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "戴笠"
			desc = "POLITICS_DAI_CHUNFENG_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Dai_Chunfeng.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = tot_kleptocracy_subtype
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name =  HNN_totalist_party_proc_k_long
			name =  HNN_totalist_party_proc_k
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = HNN_PROC_D
		HNN_fcations_change = yes 
		add_ideas = HNN_di_kang_de_da_zong1
		add_ideas = CHI_Dai_Chunfeng_sec_tot
	}
}

			}

				has_government = social_democrat
			}

			}

				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
	}

		tag = HNN
		has_country_flag = HNN_gong_tuan_victory_flag
		613 = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		is_neighbor_of = SHC
		SHC = {
			has_country_flag = zong_gong_hui_victory
		}
	}

			limit = {

					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			SHC = {
				country_event = { 
					id = hungong.148
					hours = 4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SHC
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SHC
					transfer_troops = yes
				}

					SHC_Sun_Fuyuan = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
					SHC_Kang_Sheng = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
					SHC_Nikolay_Kuibyshev = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
					SHC_Background_Alternate = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
					SHC_Alexander_Ivanovich_Cherepanov = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
					SHC_Rao_Shu_Shi = {
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}

		}
	}

country_event = {#初见成效
	id = hunqingxi.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hunqingxi.16" }
	title = hunqingxi.16.t
	desc = hunqingxi.16.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = HNN_ren_tou
				value = 4
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = HNN_ren_tou
				value = 7
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#继续动手
